Hong Kong Government Launches Anti-Smoking Campaign

Hong Kong, 2nd (Domei News Agency) - Governor Isogai told Chinese newspaper reporters today that the Hong Kong government has recently launched an anti-smoking campaign, the result of which will be to eliminate opium smoking on Hong Kong Island within the next ten years. The purpose of the Hong Kong government's promulgation of the anti-smoking ordinance is to eliminate the poisonous atmosphere. The daily amount of opium smoked by opium smokers will be gradually reduced, until there are no opium smokers in Hong Kong within ten years. Governor Isogai also revealed that a plan is now being drawn up to invite Japanese doctors with experience in opium problems to Hong Kong to assist in completely banning smoking.

National Government Orders Removal of Yellow Markings Added to National Flag; Effective from the 5th of this Month

Nanjing, 2nd (Central News Agency) - Since the return of the National Government to the capital, a yellow triangular mark with the words "Peace, Anti-Communism, Nation Building" has been added to the top of the national flag for identification. Now, in order to participate in the Greater East Asia War, cooperate with Japan, and defeat the common enemies of British and American aggression, the situation has further developed. Therefore, a clear order is issued to remove all yellow triangular marks added to the top of the national flag from the 5th of this month. However, for the front-line troops who need to add identification to the flags used in contact with the Chongqing puppet regime, the Military Commission will formulate temporary measures separately. The original text of the National Government's order is recorded below:

Since the return of the National Government to the capital, a yellow triangular mark with the words "Peace, Anti-Communism, Nation Building" has been added to the top of the national flag for identification. Now, with the efforts of compatriots and comrades, the situation has further developed, adhering to the legacy of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Great Asianism, participating in the Greater East Asia War, and cooperating with Japan to defeat the common enemies of British and American aggression, therefore, a clear order is issued to remove all yellow triangular marks added to the top of the national flag from the 5th of this month. For the front-line troops who need to add identification to the flags used in contact with the Chongqing puppet regime, the Military Commission will formulate temporary measures separately. All our citizens should jointly recognize the mission of the times, work hard to complete the great cause of revitalizing China and defending East Asia, and encourage each other not to neglect this order. Chairman Wang Zhaoming of the National Government.

Chinese and Japanese Armies Cooperate in South China to Attack Mao Feng Mountain; Defeating Chongqing Troops in Two Days

Guangzhou, 2nd (Domei News Agency) - Chinese National Government troops and the Japanese dispatch army in South China have recently been cooperating closely with local patrol units to carry out suppression operations against Chongqing troops in Guangdong Province. This will greatly benefit the combat training of the National Government troops. On January 6, the joint forces launched an encirclement operation against the Chongqing troops entrenched in the areas around Mao Feng Mountain in central Guangdong Province. It was completed within two days, and then a sudden attack was launched to annihilate the Chongqing troops and capture various spoils of war, including 504 rifles, 9,500 rounds of ammunition, 120 pistols, and two cannons. During the operation, local officials and people voluntarily cooperated with the joint Chinese and Japanese forces. The people who evacuated at the beginning of the campaign have now returned home one after another, indicating that the entire area is now safe. In order to enhance the effectiveness of the Chinese patrol army in maintaining public order in the area, the Japanese army has donated all the spoils of war.

Jinan, 2nd (Central News Agency) - Since the 9th of this month, the Japanese army in northern Shandong has launched suppression operations in the lower reaches of the old Yellow River in northern Shandong. They are still sweeping up the remaining communist troops in the east-southeast of Liyi and the south of Linyi, and also carrying out suppression operations around Wudingdao. The comprehensive battle results confirmed since the beginning of the war until the 30th are as follows: 938 communist troops were left dead, Pang Xiangwu, commander of the Second Military District of the communist army in the surrounding area of Jilu, was killed in battle, 463 people were captured, and the Japanese army intercepted a large number of military supplies.

Jinan, 2nd (Central News Agency) - On the dawn of the 28th, the Japanese army's punitive expeditionary force went to the northeastern region of Linxiong, Shandong Province, to suppress about 180 troops of the Chongqing army's Gong Ziying unit. After two hours of fighting, they were defeated, and the results were as follows: the Chongqing army abandoned 45 corpses, 16 people were captured, and 35 rifles, 26 rounds of ammunition, and 35 hand grenades were seized.

Xuzhou, 2nd (Central News Agency) - In order to help establish the current state of security, the Japanese army in the Suhuai area continued to carry out sweeping operations in the area day and night, regardless of the severe cold. Second Anniversary of the Establishment of the East Asia League; Speech by Director Lin; The East Asia League and the Greater East Asia War

Nanjing, 2nd (Central News Agency) - The 1st was the second anniversary of the establishment of the China General Association of the East Asia League. The Central Broadcasting Station specially invited Lin Bosheng, Director of the Propaganda Committee of the Association, to broadcast a speech entitled "The East Asia League and the Greater East Asia War." He first stated that two years after the signing of the Sino-Japanese Treaty, according to the spirit of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Great Asianism and the spirit of the Sino-Japanese Basic Relations Treaty, the China General Association of the East Asia League was established to launch the East Asia League ideological movement. After one year, the Greater East Asia War broke out, and the East Asia League movement changed from ideology to fact. After another year, the National Government resolutely joined the war, which further proved that our promotion of the East Asia League was not just a kind of speech, but a concrete action to achieve its realization. He then stated that a small number of people misunderstand the Greater East Asia War as a struggle between Japan and Britain and the United States in the Pacific, which is a great mistake. At the beginning of the peace movement, friendly countries advocated the construction of a new order in East Asia. The Sino-Japanese Treaty and the Three-Power Declaration clearly stated "the construction of a new order in East Asia based on the spirit of morality." The so-called new order, the so-called spirit of morality, is the meaning of the Greater East Asia War, and also the foundation of the East Asia League. In other words, the Greater East Asia War is a war of the spirit of morality against hegemonicism and colonialism, and the combination of aggressive powers is a combination of utilitarianism. The East Asia League is a permanent combination based on the spirit of morality. Finally, he said that the Greater East Asia War is not just a military struggle. In the economic, political, and cultural aspects, a thorough struggle must be launched. Not only must we use force to drive out the aggressive forces of Britain and the United States in East Asia, but also overthrow the political, economic, and cultural systems of British and American utilitarianism. At the same time, in the positive aspect, we must establish new political, economic, cultural, and military systems based on the spirit of morality, replace colonialism with the principle of a co-prosperity sphere, and replace utilitarianism with the spirit of morality, so that the East Asian nations can, within the East Asian Co-Prosperity Sphere, build a new East Asian order based on the spirit of morality according to the four major guidelines of political independence, economic cooperation, military alliance, and cultural communication of the East Asia League. On the second anniversary of the establishment of the China General Association of the East Asia League, we recall with the greatest sincerity and encourage all compatriots to work together under the four major guidelines of the East Asia League and with the spirit of the New National Movement to strive for the Greater East Asia War, completely revive China, and defend the mission of East Asia.

British and American Anxiety Over the Difficulty of Counter-Offensives

-Sakura

The lingering pain of New Guinea still lingers, German submarines are difficult to deal with

"Lisbon Special Telegram 24th dispatched by Sakura Special Correspondent" - The Soviet counter-offensive, the retreat of Rommel's army, and the British military commentators with agreed propaganda materials, have produced optimistic arguments. But there are still two real problems to consider. First, the threat of submarines, American assistance in materials and personnel is absolutely necessary for Britain, and this is also the key to victory or defeat, without American assistance, attacking Europe will be a dream. The activities of Axis submarines in all the world's oceans are becoming more and more aggressive. The revised Roth wartime insurance rates on the 16th listed the northern waters of the United Kingdom and the area near Malta in the western Mediterranean as outside the scope of coverage, indicating that these sea areas are considered the most dangerous places. The insurance rate for the Atlantic route from the United Kingdom to the Americas and the west coast of Africa has increased to 10%, the United Kingdom via the Cape of Good Hope to Australia to 15%, the United Kingdom to the Red Sea, Aden, Suez, Port Said, Alexandria to Malta to 20%, and the United Kingdom via the Cape of Good Hope and the Red Sea to Syria to 17%, and to Turkey to 20%.

Military commentator Harky said in the Sunday Times: "More submarines are being built than sunk, but half of the ships lost by the British and Americans this year cannot digest the attacking power with their transportation capacity." Emmanuel said in the Daily Express: "The German submarine according to the Secretary of the Navy has 500 ships, but in fact there are probably more than this number. Since the beginning of the war, the losses of the British and Americans have exceeded the total tonnage of Britain in 1935. Even if the United States builds a lot of ships, if there are no fast and defensive cargo ships, escort warships, and escort aircraft, the shipbuilding plan will eventually be disappointed."

Although experts have various countermeasures for submarines, they are nothing more than bombing submarine factories, naval and air force escorts, and building fast cargo ships. Because none of these can achieve absolute results, it is impossible to decide which strategy to focus on. The results of bombing the factories did not reduce the production of submarines as the government claimed. In short, without a proper solution, the threat posed by submarine tactics in this war is far greater than in the last war.

Another problem is that the land battles in New Guinea have made the difficulty of fighting Japan even more painful. A special correspondent from The Times reported, saying that the Japanese army is strong, unafraid of death, and difficult to attack. The newspaper's editorial on the 14th advocated that a policy of piecemeal destruction should not be adopted, but that all efforts should be made to defeat Japan first. The editorial argued: "Sea power depends on air power, and air power depends on land power. If airfields are opened in China to carry out large-scale air strikes, Japan will immediately occupy them with its army. Therefore, at this time, when fighting Japan, strong land forces should be placed in Burma and the Pacific, and the air force should launch attacks from Burma to attack transport ships in the Pacific." Both newspapers simultaneously opposed making the continents the first battlefield and the Orient the second battlefield, and warned against the general battle theory of defeating Germany first and then attacking Japan, and downplaying the mistake of Japan. Due to the losses of huge warships and lives in the battle of New Guinea last year, a major warning was given. In order to defeat Japan, this kind of war should no longer be continued in the future, and it advocated regaining East Bengal Bay, reopening the Burma Road to assist the Chongqing army, and attacking Japan. The Sunday Times said on the 17th:

"This is the most correct argument. We are too far away from Japan to understand Japan. The only ones who can attack Japan are the Soviet Union, but the Soviet Union has not yet joined the war with Japan. The biggest obstacles to the offensive theory are submarines and the Japanese army, and this is also the aim of the Axis powers." (翔: Translated from the Tokyo Mainichi Shimbun on January 27th)

Japanese Air Force Active in Southern China

Nanjing, 2nd (Central News Agency) - According to a telegram from a certain frontline base of the Japanese army, the Yu army, which raided key points such as Shaoguan, Guilin, and Yong'an, has suffered severe bombing by the Japanese air force. Its troop strength and military facilities in these areas have been almost completely destroyed. In order to regroup and make a comeback, they are attempting to stir up trouble. In order to thoroughly punish them, the Japanese air force continues to bomb the Yu army's bases in the Xijiang and Beijiang areas. They also repeatedly attacked the Yu army units advancing in spite of the bad weather. The following is a record of the activities of the Japanese air force from the 26th of last month to the 1st of this month. On the 26th, a bomber squadron attacked Wengyuan, 60 kilometers southeast of Shaoguan, and severely bombed the barracks of the 156th Division of the Yu army, 4 kilometers northwest of the city, destroying 60 houses. In addition, it bombed military facilities south of the city. Another squadron attacked Zhaoqing, dropping heavy bombs on the headquarters of the 64th Army of the Yu army and its military facilities. On the 27th, it attacked Heyuan, 70 kilometers northeast of Huizhou, severely damaging Yu military facilities. On the 30th, it again attacked Zhaoqing from the air, destroying the Yu army headquarters there. Another squadron attacked Fogang, kilometers east of Shaoguan, destroying six Yu army barracks. On the 31st, it attacked Qingyuan from the air, severely bombing the headquarters of the 159th Division of the Yu army. Another squadron attacked Huizhou, dropping many bombs on warehouses along the coast, causing a large fire. On the 1st, the Japanese air force flew at low altitude in spite of the bad weather, attacked Qingyuan, and severely bombed it. It also discovered about 300 Yu army soldiers marching near Sicheng Road, 25 kilometers south of the city. They were immediately pursued and machine-gunned, and completely wiped out.

Prison Names in Various Provinces Changed to Local Place Names

Nanjing, 2nd (Central News Agency) - The new prisons in various provinces under the Ministry of Judicial Administration have been named with the order of establishment, such as the First and Second Prisons of a certain province. This has been the case for a long time without change. However, since the incident, some prisons in various provinces have been destroyed by war and cannot be restored. Those that are restored later still use the original names, resulting in situations such as Jiangsu province having no First or Second Prison, but having the Third Prison, and Anhui province having only the Second Prison, but no First Prison. The order is reversed, and the names do not match the reality. In view of this, the Ministry has made corrections, canceling the First and Second, etc., names of the prisons in various provinces and changing them to the place names where they are located, in order to make them uniform. The matter has been reported to the Executive Yuan for record yesterday, and instructions have been issued to the high courts of various provinces to instruct the prisons under their jurisdiction to comply. The following is an excerpt of the corrected names: The Third Prison of Jiangsu is changed to Suzhou Prison of Jiangsu, the branch prison of the Third Prison of Jiangsu is changed to Suzhou Prison Branch of Jiangsu, the Fourth Prison of Jiangsu is changed to Nantong Prison of Jiangsu, the Fifth Prison of Jiangsu is changed to Wuxi Prison of Jiangsu, the Sixth Prison of Jiangsu is changed to Zhenjiang Prison of Jiangsu, the First Prison of Zhejiang is changed to Hangzhou Prison of Zhejiang, the Third Prison of Anhui is changed to Wuhu Prison of Anhui, the First Prison of Hubei is changed to Hankou Prison of Hubei, the branch prison of the First Prison of Hubei is changed to Hankou Prison Branch of Hubei, the First Prison of Jiangxi is changed to Jiujiang Prison of Jiangxi.

Establishment of the Ministry of Food: Minister Gu Talks About Policy Guidelines

Central News Agency, Beijing - The Ministry of Food was officially established on February 1st. Minister Gu Baochong announced his assumption of office at the same time and made an important speech on the policy guidelines of the Ministry of Food in the future. The main points are as follows: The National Government has established the Food Administration Commission for two years now. It first implemented management from the aspects of purchasing rice and distributing food to the people. Because there are other competent authorities for improving agriculture and increasing production, the Food Administration Commission did not take this into account. Now that it has been reorganized into a ministry, it will transition to the stage of overall management. From production to consumption, from main food grains to non-staple foods and substitutes, they will be guided and adjusted separately. When necessary, control will be implemented. The purpose of the Ministry's administration can be summarized as: making the best use of people's talents, land, and resources, enriching national reserves, and stabilizing people's livelihoods, thereby increasing the strength of the Greater East Asia War. According to the scope of food under the jurisdiction of the Ministry, in a broad sense, it includes not only rice, wheat, and flour, which are the main food grains in agricultural products, but also other non-staple foods such as miscellaneous grains, fish, meat, vegetables, eggs, and beverages such as tea, wine, soda, and seasonings such as oil, sauce, sugar, vinegar, etc. All those that can be used as food and are related to nutrition are included. However, salt is still under the jurisdiction of the Ministry of Finance due to tax relations. Among the main agricultural food grain management affairs, production policy is the most important, in other words, the issue of increasing production. It is now planned to first plan and implement facilities for the overall improvement of farmland, the widespread establishment of agricultural improvement experimental areas, the replenishment of seeds and fertilizers, the increase of agricultural tools and plowing cattle, the assistance of rural economy, the restoration of wasteland, the repair of dikes and ditches, and the breeding of livestock, the improvement and addition of food factories, etc., to promote the increase of wartime food production.

Regarding the strengthening of management, all manufacturers and vendors will be organized in order to promote the implementation of planned economic policies. Subsequently, it is planned to strictly implement the registration and licensing system to guide the organization of legitimate and systematic commercial groups. All legitimate merchants will be given practical protection to restore and increase the vitality of merchants. Speculation and black market trading will be cracked down on in order to thoroughly control and strengthen the guidance of general price reduction. Regarding distribution and consumption, in this extraordinary period, fairness and thrift are the first priorities. It is necessary to be consistent from top to bottom, work hard and be self-reliant, and at the same time, maintain adequate nutrition and avoid waste, in order to jointly overcome today's difficulties. From the government's standpoint, it must enable the general public to obtain various foods within the necessary limits at reasonable prices. In order to achieve this goal, in addition to requiring the public to help each other sincerely and promote self-awareness, the government will implement a ticket system when necessary. For example, essential oils and other items will be implemented in the same way as the rice ration method implemented in Beijing.

In short, today's food administration is extremely important and complex. I have been ordered to preside over it, and I vow to work carefully and diligently with all my colleagues in order to live up to the heavy trust of the country and the ardent expectations of the people. As for the rice and grain business handled by the Food Administration Commission in the past, a General Management Office for Rice and Grain Procurement and Sales has been specifically established to manage and operate it independently and continuously. This is where the nature of the Ministry and the former Food Administration Commission are slightly different.

Federal Reserve Notes and Japanese Yen Maintain Parity

Beijing, 2nd (Central News Agency) - When the Director of the Economic Affairs Bureau No. 1 of the Beijing Office of the Japanese Embassy in China met with a group of reporters a few days ago, he talked about the recent currency issue in North China. The main points were that the principle of parity between the yen (Japanese yen) and the yuan (Federal Reserve Note) will be maintained from beginning to end. It is true that various contradictions have arisen in economic policy due to the parity between the yen and the yuan, but abandoning the principle of maintaining parity will lower the value of the currency in North China, which is also not a good solution. The problem in the future lies in how to eliminate these contradictions, promote the exchange of materials, and revitalize industry. All this must be based on the solution of the price problem. In this regard, the North China Political Affairs Commission should strive to strengthen its financial strength and improve its political strength.

Shen Bao Readers' Scholarship Fund: Committee Meeting Held Yesterday, Resolved to Pay Tribute to People Who are Familiar with Helping Students, Encourage All Selected Students to Cultivate Morality and Study Hard

The review and verification procedures for the university group and the industrial and commercial organizations have also come to an end. Therefore, a scholarship fund committee meeting was held at this newspaper yesterday to decide on various important matters related to this year's scholarship. All the committee members were concerned about the students and gave many instructions. The details are recorded as follows:

Summary Report of Handling Affairs

The Scholarship Fund Committee met at 4:00 p.m. yesterday. The attending committee members were Mr. Shen Siliang, Mr. Chen Qingshi, Mr. Lu Gaoyi, Mr. Zhao Zongyu, Ms. Nie Yu (represented by Chen), and more than ten colleagues from the scholarship fund office of this newspaper. First, the colleagues from this newspaper reported on the scholarship situation this year: (1) The students who applied for the scholarship and participated in the examinations this year were: (A) 84 students in grades 5 and 6 of primary school; (B) 1634 students in junior and senior high school; (C) 215 university students; (D) 60 students in the industrial and commercial group. (2) As of today, the scholarship funds received from all sectors this year total 254,739.40 yuan. In terms of the enthusiastic donations, we should thank all sectors. In terms of the number of students applying for scholarships, which is more than 2,700, we still feel that we cannot provide universal assistance. (3) More than 2,400 primary and secondary school students this year were entrusted to the male and female youth associations to conduct the examinations, which was extremely hard work. We would like to express our gratitude. (4) This year, a total of 18 primary and secondary schools sent letters to support this newspaper's scholarship movement and donate funds. (5) Mr. Zeng Gongye, Mr. Pu Qiting, and Mr. Dai Cangqi, who are lonely and suffering in their old age, have either donated clothes or paintings to help students, and their enthusiasm is commendable.

Key Resolutions - Totaling Ten Items

Subsequently, various proposals were discussed: (1) The committee believes that all sectors have enthusiastically supported this newspaper's scholarship movement and should express sincere gratitude. (2) Approved the list of students approved for scholarship funds at all levels of primary and secondary schools. (3) Resolved that the list of students approved for scholarships in the university group and the industrial and commercial group will be approved and announced at the next meeting. (4) Madam Yao Zhao's will to help students, the funds collected by this school on behalf of all sectors totaling more than 19,000 yuan, and the proposal by the Yao family to establish a separate fund committee were resolved to be approved and transferred to the fund committee to handle scholarship matters. (5) Mr. Gu Dingfu, Jing'an Temple, Female Youth Association, and Mr. Zhu Yiyun of Dacheng Xinsheng Silk Factory sent letters stating that they either designated the funds or requested that the selection procedures be handled on their behalf in installments. Resolved that this newspaper's scholarship fund should continue to be handled in accordance with the past policy. We are extremely grateful to those who enthusiastically donate funds and should handle them separately in accordance with the regulations. (6) Resolved to continue to approve the various fees for disaster-stricken children this semester. (7) Resolved to liberally approve the scholarship funds for students whose families are particularly poor. (8) Resolved to provide assistance as much as possible to students in the sixth grade of primary school, the third grade of junior and senior high school, and the third grade of university who are applying for scholarships and are only one semester away from graduation, in order to complete their studies. (9) Resolved to supervise the studies of all students who have been approved for scholarships in the past and continue to provide assistance as much as possible. (10) Students who failed the examination this year will be re-examined on a regular basis. Based on the principles resolved in cases 7, 8, and 9, in addition to the students who are approved for scholarship funds this year, the remaining funds will be allocated for assistance.

Hope That Students Cultivate Morality and Study Hard

The committee members, in the midst of their busy official duties, braved the wind and rain to attend the meeting at this newspaper yesterday. Committee members Chen, Lu, and Shen gave detailed guidance and encouragement to the colleagues on the future scholarship work, and their sincere concern for the situation of poor students and their kind words are always the original intention of people from all walks of life to donate funds. The committee members believe that the amount of scholarship funds collected from all sectors this year, during this period of general business closure, is a testament to the courage of the social people to do good and promote the spirit of human mutual assistance, which is very valuable. In addition, the committee members also hope that the assisted students will cultivate morality and become capable talents, so as not to disappoint the expectations of all sectors for scholarship assistance.

Junior High School List to Be Announced Today

The list of students approved for scholarships in junior high school will be announced in this newspaper starting today, in order to avoid the students waiting for the announcement. The procedures for the funds are being rushed, and a notice will be issued later. It is hoped that the students will bring their registration certificate and the seal that matches the one used when applying, and come to the newspaper in person to receive the funds on time.

Due to the current situation, the company announced its dissolution, and all the remaining funds, totaling 849.48 yuan in national currency, were donated to your newspaper's loan scholarship fund after the committee's resolution. Now, our company has saved 400 yuan from the Lunar New Year's banquet expenses and donated it to this year's scholarship fund. It is a drop in the bucket, but it expresses our sincere intentions.

Meeting of Japanese Administrative Officials This Morning: Discussing Resident Association Finances and Drafting Guidelines for the Support the War Effort Movement

Dispatch from Allied News Agency, Shanghai: According to news last night, Japanese administrative officials from Central and Southern China are scheduled to meet at the Astor House Hotel in Shanghai at 10:00 this morning to discuss the budget of the Japanese Residents Association for the fiscal year 1943-44 and to draft guidelines for the Support the War Effort Movement for Japanese nationals in China. This is the first gathering of officials from Japanese consulates in China this year. The first meeting was held on January 20 to discuss modifications to Japanese policies towards China after the Nanjing government joined the war. The second meeting is hosted by the Shanghai office of the Japanese Embassy and will be attended by Yano, the Consul-General in Shanghai, as well as officials and representatives from Japanese consulates throughout Central and Southern China.

Reader's Forum

Request for Metered Grain Distribution for the City District

— 3rd installment

The metered grain distribution of the concession authorities, with ten days as a period, ordered the rice shops to sell, never failing to do so on time, and there was never any difference in the quality and price of the rice sold by each rice shop during the same period of metered grain distribution. Looking back at the metered grain distribution in the city district, it is completely different. It has never been possible to distribute it on time. Delays pile on delays, and the three installments per month are completely delayed and vanish without a trace. Moreover, within the same period of so-called metered grain distribution, there are often differences in price and rice quality. As a resident of the Nanshi district, I am very familiar with the metered grain distribution in Nanshi, having personally experienced it. I would like to describe it in detail so that the relevant authorities can understand the general situation and implore the City Grain Administration Bureau to sympathize with the people's plight and improve the system.

For the first month or two, the metered grain distribution in Nanshi was actually household-based, not individual-based, with each household receiving one dou of rice per period, without a fixed schedule. It was not until October of last year that individual-based metered grain distribution was implemented. However, the three installments of grain that should have been received in mid-October were not issued until the end of November. The quantity was also reduced from two sheng of white rice per person per period to one sheng and five ge of broken rice per person per period. One installment in between was supplemented with one jin of flour per person. The November installment was delayed until early December, with 1.4 sheng of brown rice per person (another ge of rice less), and the half jin of flour per person missing from the second installment in October was provided as a supplement. Later, on December 25, the second installment for November was issued, totaling 1.4 sheng of white and broken rice. The third installment for November was not distributed until January 7 of this year, with 1.4 sheng of white rice and 1.5 jin of flour. Afterwards, the rice tickets were changed, effectively canceling the December installment, and the rice tickets received were the three-part rice and flour tickets for January of the 32nd year of the Republic. The first part, the rice ticket, was used to receive two sheng of brown rice per person on January 20 (according to the household rice issued in the first and second wards, it was 1.6 ge of white rice and 4 ge of broken rice per person, costing five yuan, while in the third ward where I live, it was purely brown rice, and the selling price was one jiao more expensive, at 5.1 yuan per person). The second part, the grain ticket, was used to distribute 1.8 sheng of white rice per person on January 30 (another two ge of rice less than the previous installment), costing 4.6 yuan. As of February 2, there has been no news of the distribution of the third installment, and the three-part flour ticket has not yet been issued. Originally, the household rice was not enough to maintain the minimum needs of an individual. Now, the city district's distribution is much less in quantity than that of the two concessions, and there is no flour to supplement it. Moreover, it is often delayed and canceled altogether. Therefore, all the innocent people in our million-strong city district are craning their necks and longing, hoping that our city district authorities will quickly improve the situation to help our million starving people. I believe that our wise city district authorities will be able to understand the feelings of the people and make some gestures. At the very least, they should be able to effectively implement the following points in the shortest possible time:

(1) Determine the date of grain distribution. (2) Supplement each installment with flour. (3) Ensure that the quality, price, and quantity of rice are the same in all districts. (4) Order all rice shops not to deliberately create difficulties.

The Second Voice, He Lan

Your newspaper's loud call for attention to the food problem has obviously achieved considerable results. Isn't the ration of household rice and household flour increasing installment by installment? Although the current ration is still not enough to meet all the needs, the severity of the food problem has gradually decreased with the increase in the ration. But this is referring to the two concessions. As for our Shanghai Fourth District, the food problem is still very serious. At the same time, the grain administration authorities seem to think that everyone can still buy 1.5 sheng of white rice, 6 ge of brown rice, 7 ge of broken rice, and 1.5 jin of flour. Today, the rice purchase certificate was finally issued, but each person is only allowed to buy 7 ge of white rice, 1.1 sheng of brown rice, and 2 ge of broken rice. In total, each person will buy 2.2 sheng of white rice, 1.7 sheng of brown rice, 9 ge of broken rice, and 1.5 jin of flour this month. I ask, how many days will this amount of food last one person? This problem is serious enough in normal times, let alone now that the authorities have issued a ban prohibiting the free entry of food, which naturally makes the problem even more acute. Although the Shanghai West District is not without wealthy families, the hidden poor and the destitute still account for the majority, no, they account for the vast majority. I have an income of one thousand and several hundred yuan per month, and the organization I serve allows me to buy 1.35 dou of specially rationed rice per month, but in recent months, there has not been a single month where I have not spent more than I earned, resulting in borrowing and pawning. I examined my accounts and found that most of the money was spent on supplementing food. Now, the black market rice is more expensive and not easy to buy. If the grain ration cannot be increased, then I simply cannot live. I think there must be many residents in the Shanghai West District who are in the same situation as me, or even worse. The threat they face from the food problem can naturally be imagined. On behalf of the 1.5 million residents of the Shanghai West District, I earnestly hope that the grain administration authorities in the Shanghai West District can understand the difficulty of the people's food and quickly achieve the following two points:

(1) Issue another 1.2 sheng of rice and 4.2 jin of flour per person this month. This, together with what has been issued before, is exactly equal to the quantity distributed by the two concessions in one month.

(2) From February onwards, the method and frequency of monthly distribution, and the quantity of each distribution, should be exactly the same as in the two concessions.

I believe that what the authorities of the two concessions can do, the grain administration authorities of the Shanghai West District can certainly do as well. I also believe that the grain administration party authorities in the Shanghai West District must be no less concerned about maintaining the people's food supply than the authorities in the two concessions. I hereby express my sincere hope!

The Third Voice

Since the strict control of the grain administration was implemented on January 13, street vendors and rice merchants have almost disappeared from the market, and rice and noodle shops are all out of stock. The citizens are eager for household rice, but it cannot be distributed according to the same schedule as in the concessions. There are rumors of increasing the ration, but the most recent installment in the city district has actually been reduced. The first installment of household rice in January was not issued until the 21st, with 2 sheng per person, and the second installment was issued on the 29th, with 1.8 sheng per person, without any flour. There is still no news of the third installment. According to the ration in the concessions, it is only enough for five days, while in the city district, each person has only received 3.8 sheng in the two installments this month, making it impossible for people to eat their fill. The authorities implemented strict control originally to suppress the black market and benefit the people, but like an elastic, the black market is becoming more entrenched and the resilience is higher. (Chen Jie)

Temporary Extension for Purchasing Gunny Sacks; Overdue Violators Will Be Penalized and Confiscated: Announcement by the Office of the Japanese Embassy

The office of the Japanese Embassy in Shanghai, in view of the peak season for agricultural products and to ensure the supply of gunny sacks for packaging agricultural products, had previously consulted with the municipal government, the Public Works Department, and the Public Works Bureau to purchase gunny sacks stored in the city. However, the purchase period was very short, and the purpose of the authorities' purchase had not been fully understood by the general public. Therefore, the purchase period has been extended to February 13. It is hoped that the citizens will cooperate. Those who miss the deadline again and fail to sell to the authorities will be confiscated, and the owners will be severely punished. The office of the Japanese Embassy has recently issued the following statement regarding this matter: "Our embassy office previously consulted with the municipal government, the Public Works Department, and the Public Works Bureau to implement the purchase of gunny sacks stored in the city, as you citizens are aware. The results of the purchase have been very smooth recently. However, because the purchase period is very short and the methods for informing the citizens have not been thorough, there are likely many who have not fully understood the details of this plan. Therefore, the municipal authorities have decided to extend the deadline to February 13. During this extended period, the purchase method will be the same as before. We will not take coercive measures. It is hoped that the citizens will cooperate voluntarily. If the expected goal is not achieved during this period, then the three municipal authorities will take coercive measures such as confiscation for any gunny sacks found thereafter, regardless of the circumstances. We sincerely hope that the citizens understand that this purchase plan will achieve significant results in the restoration of Shanghai and the reconstruction of Central China. We hope that everyone will take the lead in cooperating with the authorities to avoid coercive measures that are not originally intended by the authorities and are also extremely dishonorable for all citizens."

Women's Welfare Association Seeks Members

Since its establishment on the 29th of last month, the Shanghai Women's Welfare Association has spared no effort in promoting its affairs. In order to expand its organization, it has started publishing advertisements on the 1st to openly solicit members. Intellectual women from all walks of life are welcome to participate enthusiastically. It is said that the procedures are very simple. The association's address is No. 984, Lane 972, at the intersection of Jing'an Temple Road and Muir Ming Road. Registration hours are from 2:00 pm to 5:00 pm, Monday to Friday. Latecomers will not be entertained.

Central Reserve Bank to Move to New Location

Before the August 13th Incident, the Bank of China started constructing a new building on the Bund. However, due to the outbreak of the incident, the construction was interrupted. Later, the Central Reserve Bank hired workers to continue the construction of the new building, which has now been completed. Therefore, the Central Reserve Bank will soon move into the new building to conduct its business.

Retail Sales Tax May Not Be Exempted; Invoices Must Be Issued for All Purchases, Regardless of Amount

The Public Works Department of the Public Concession and the Public Works Bureau of the French Concession stipulated that all companies and merchants must collect a 2% retail sales tax when selling goods at retail. Since its implementation, the results have been remarkable. It is now learned that some shops sometimes exempt this retail sales tax, which is a violation of the law. Therefore, special personnel will be dispatched to investigate at any time. Any merchant who sells goods, if they are indeed retail sales, must collect the retail sales tax in accordance with the law and may not freely exempt it. Otherwise, if discovered, they will be severely punished according to the law. At the same time, all retailers must issue invoices for the sale of goods, regardless of the amount, so that the authorities can review whether the amount of goods sold is consistent with the retail sales tax collected.

Final Settlement Period for the Banking Industry; Ticket Collection Hours Remain the Same; Chinese New Year is Approaching, Work is Tense

All banks and money shops in the city's banking industry are particularly busy with the final settlement procedures for the end of the lunar year, as the deadline is approaching. Although it is impossible to find the exact amount of all ticket exchanges, customer account receipts, and interbank lending figures, they have increased more than twice as much as in the previous week. The work of each bank, shop, the Banking Association, the clearing house, the Money Industry Reserve, the Money Industry Market, and other aspects has been very tense, and the office hours seem to have been extended. In the concentrated areas of banks and shops, the personnel for collecting accounts and remitting funds are coming and going frequently. The reporter learned from the financial sector yesterday that the ticket collection time for the final settlement of the money industry will not be changed, as the association decided at the executive committee meeting last time to wait for consultation with the Banking Association before issuing a notice for compliance. Now, the money industry has sent personnel to consult with the Banking Association, and the ticket collection time for the two industries has been decided to remain unchanged, with the time ending at 4:00 pm. The external business and office hours and the return time for tickets have also been decided to remain unchanged. It is reported that the interbank foreign exchange rate of the money industry was reduced to 1.4 jiao yesterday.

Councilor Okazaki Comes to Shanghai to Promote Economic Measures; Conveys the Intentions of the Greater East Asia Ministry to Various Agencies; Will Consult with Economic Giants of China and Japan on Various Issues

Okazaki Kahira, Councilor of the Greater East Asia Ministry, came to Shanghai via North China to promote the economic measures of the National Government participating in the war, to convey the intentions of the Greater East Asia Ministry to various agencies stationed in China, and to consult with relevant parties on important matters. He arrived in Shanghai on the 1st and stayed at the Whiteaway Laidlaw Building. Okazaki met with Okuda, the Minister of Economic Affairs at the Shanghai Office of the Embassy that day and had some discussions. He will also consult with economic giants of China and Japan on various economic issues.

Brief Commentary

Concessions Increase Household Rice

Increasing the quantity of household rice has been a unanimous demand of the people of the city. In the past, this newspaper's suggestions and the public's appeals have been repeated again and again. The authorities have also expressed deep concern about this issue. First, on January 13, they issued an order prohibiting the free transfer of food, in order to uniformly purchase food from the interior and transport it to Shanghai for distribution. Now, they have decided to increase the quantity of household rice, from 4.8 kilograms per person per month to 6 kilograms (i.e., from 6 sheng to 7.5 sheng), an increase of a quarter. The increased quantity may not yet meet the needs, but it is enough to prove that the authorities can value public opinion and adopt the people's will. Here, on the one hand, we firmly believe that the authorities will continue to find ways to increase it to the most basic quantity per person as soon as possible; on the other hand, we thank the authorities for their concern for the people's suffering. At the same time, now that the concessions have decided to increase, we also hope that the food authorities in the city district will quickly plan to improve the situation, as this newspaper has repeatedly received reports from readers in the city district (see this newspaper's Reader's Forum today) that the ration quantity is less than that of the concessions, and the distribution dates are not accurate.

Central Reserve Bank Moves to New Location

The Central Reserve Bank will soon move into the former Bank of China's new location to conduct business. Before August 13, the Bank of China was building a large building on Nanking Road and the Bund, but the construction was interrupted due to the incident. After the outbreak of the Greater East Asia War, the building was regarded as enemy property and managed by the Japanese army. Now it has been returned to the National Government and designated for use by the Central Reserve Bank. This move by the Japanese authorities aims to assist the development of the Central Reserve Bank. How the bank will operate well in the future to consolidate finance, strengthen the wartime economy, and fulfill the mission of the national bank is something we eagerly look forward to.

More Than One Hundred Groups Registered with the Public Works Department Have Been Approved and Given Certificates

Since the Public Association Department of the Public Works Department Police Headquarters was established and ordered all industrial and commercial groups and trade associations within the concession to apply for registration, the deadline has expired. It is reported that a total of 422 groups have registered, and 124 units have been issued certificates for establishment. The rest are still under strict review.

The Income Tax Office of the Ministry of Finance Intensifies the Collection of Profit Tax; Orders Subordinates to Compile a Merchant Register

Since the income tax of the Ministry of Finance has been levied, the tax collection has been on the right track. However, there are still many who do not declare and pay taxes. In order to increase tax revenue and prevent tax evasion, the Ministry of Finance has decided to intensify the collection of profit income tax for the first category of Class A and B profit-making enterprises. It has been ordered to compile a merchant register for verification. A notice has been sent to the tax collection bureaus in each district to send personnel to investigate the addresses, capital amounts, and profit status of each company, shop, and factory in the district and to start compiling a merchant register. Unified bookkeeping is also being implemented to facilitate verification and report taxes on profit income as accurately as possible. The compilation of the merchant register must be completed before the end of March of this year and reported for approval.

The First Batch of Standard Water Ladles Is Temporarily Limited to Use in the City District; The Two Concessions Will Set a Separate Date for Issuance

The Shanghai Boiled Water Shop Association was previously notified by the Metrology and Testing Office of the Social Bureau that all water ladles used by the boiled water shops must be in accordance with the 1000cc standard capacity to standardize them and must be replaced within a limited time. After receiving the order, the association immediately produced a batch of standard water ladles and began issuing them in late last month. It is learned that the issuance of the first batch of water ladles is temporarily limited to the city district members, while the members in the two concessions are waiting for a separate date.

Selection of Students for the Central Youth Cadre School; Initial Test Results Announced in Shanghai

The selection of the second batch of students for the Central Youth Cadre School in Shanghai was entrusted to the Shanghai Special City Branch of the New National Movement Promotion Committee, and Feng Jie, a member of the school affairs committee, was appointed as the examiner. It is reported that the New Movement Committee Shanghai Branch has been actively conducting the selection process. The initial test was held at the association on January 30, and the participants were very enthusiastic. The test papers have now been graded, and the students who have been admitted are Chen Zhuhua, Huang Boxi, Fang Yan, Zhang Zhibiao, Huang Wenqing, and Wang Yiqiao. The admitted students will complete all the procedures from the 3rd to the 7th of this month and will go to Beijing on the 8th to participate in the school's re-examination.

Public Works Department, Industrial and Social Affairs Department Report for January

Last month, several rubber factories that had stopped work previously resumed work, and many small chemical factories were established, manufacturing chemicals to replace imported goods. The bleaching powder factory business was not as good as before. The coffee essence factory was affected by the decline in the price of its products. Recently, the atmosphere has been dry, and the tap water contains salt, which has made the manufacturing of the products quite difficult.

Ensuring Safety

The Bureau's Newsletter published an announcement, ordering people who use elevators to strictly comply with the Bureau's regulations for elevator operation. Elevators must be inspected on schedule to avoid excessive crowding of passengers to ensure safety. Charcoal factories have complied with the improvement of equipment to prevent smoke leakage. There were five fire alarms in factories, but there were no deaths or injuries.

Boiler Inspection

Fourteen steam pressure machines were registered, eight boiler inspection certificates were received, and fifty-four annual re-inspections were received. Eighteen boilers were affixed with the Bureau's number. One boiler manufacturing factory owner was sentenced by the court to ten days of detention for manufacturing boilers without the supervision of a qualified engineer.

Stoker Training

Seventy-six students in the 11th Boiler Stoker Training Class received their completion certificates. The 12th Fire Training Class is located in the East District and currently has seventy-four students. The two night schools for young technicians in the East and West Districts held major exams, and the students performed well, averaging above 80 points.

Job Placement

Since its establishment, the Job Placement Section has registered 624 technicians and has introduced 127 to various factories. Among them, 27 have been hired, 31 are not suitable, and 42 are under consideration.

Dispute Resolution

The Industrial and Social Affairs Department mediated three industrial disputes, affecting 74 workers. The department convened many factory owners to discuss issues relating to wages, allowances, and the dismissal of workers.

Lost Children

The Child Protection Section handled 143 cases of children. Forty-four lost children were sent back to their families, seven were allowed to be adopted, and thirty-two were placed in special care facilities. The section plans to hold a Children's Happiness Week during the Lunar New Year to guide parents on how to prevent children from running away or getting lost.

Junior High School Approved List: Jin Ming to be published in two days. The date for collecting funds is set to begin on the 10th. It is hoped that everyone will pay attention. The lists for senior high school and university groups will be announced after the holidays.

After the Implementation of the Rationing System, the Problems of Oil and Sugar Still Remain Unresolved. A New System May Be Implemented After the Lunar New Year.

The problems of oil and sugar, two major food items in this city, have not been completely resolved recently. However, after the Lunar New Year, the supply of these two major food items will eventually have a formal solution implemented, no matter what.

Insufficient Distribution of Oil

Sensing the urgency of residents' needs during the Lunar New Year period, the wholesale office of the food oil industry held sales of oil at retail stores for the first two days of this month. However, because the ration was not large, most residents were still unable to enjoy this right. As for the automatic distribution of oil by population in some Baojia districts, it was entirely temporary in nature, and due to the cessation of rationing by the wholesale office, it eventually came to an invisible halt. Therefore, the oil industry authorities are now planning to implement a universal system of oil distribution by population, so that every resident can enjoy this major food item, so that it is not monopolized by a few people, and so that residents do not feel deeply troubled. Half a Catty of Sugar Per Person: After the Sugar Merchant Cooperative Business Office was approved by the military allocation authorities to implement sugar rationing by population, all sugar distribution rules have now been decided. It was originally scheduled to start the fourth phase on February 1st, first piloting in the Nanshi area, based on the Baojia household registration book. The cooperative business office and the Baojia authorities have agreed on assistance measures. However, due to the inability to complete the household registration book in time, it was decided to postpone it to February 10th, and purchases will be made with the sugar purchase certificates issued in advance. However, according to the reporter's inquiry, the amount of sugar rationed in the pilot program is said to be temporarily set at half a catty per person. The price will be announced by the cooperative business office according to the official price limit, so that the public can be informed. Afterwards, the allocation amount will be determined according to the population ratio based on the monthly amount approved by the military allocation authorities. If the pilot program is effective, it will be universally implemented throughout the city from the fifth phase on March 1st. Before implementation, the Public Concession, the French Concession, as well as Huxi, Hongkou, and Zhabei will temporarily issue sales based on house tax tickets, all in accordance with the newly established improvement measures.

Small-Scale Noodle Shops Have Been Given Flour Rations First

The noodle product shops and stalls in the two concessions have repeatedly submitted documents to the authorities through the guild requesting the restoration of flour rationing. It is now known that the distribution of flour to cooked noodle businesses began yesterday. However, it is limited to small-scale noodle shops of the third and fourth class. The flour for the first and second class cooked noodle shops has not been rationed. The sliced ​​noodle industry (i.e. raw noodle shops) has been closed for a long time. The day before yesterday, representatives were dispatched again to petition the competent authorities, following the cooked noodle industry, to quickly restore flour rationing to maintain livelihoods and facilitate public purchases. It is now known that the authorities are reviewing it. As for the flour rationing for the flatbread and fried dough stick industry and the cake and steamed bun industry, the flour rationing office of the Materials Control Department once convened representatives of the two industries for discussions the day before yesterday, considering that they are foods for the working class, and other remedial measures will be discussed and given priority to supply products, so as to facilitate the public in the lower classes.

The 25th Term of Rations Shortened the Purchase Period

The registered rice shops in the two concessions issued a temporary announcement yesterday, stating that the water shops have been instructed by the authorities to handle the 25th term of rations per capita starting from February 1st. All white rice will be issued at two liters and flour at one catty and twelve taels per ration ticket for 8.85 yuan. However, the sales period for this term has been shortened to seven days. The 5th and 6th of each day (the first and second days of the Lunar New Year) will be closed as usual. It is hoped that citizens holding tickets will come to purchase them as soon as possible. Once the deadline is exceeded, it will be regarded as self-abandonment, and the rice flour ticket will not be used. We hope that all sectors pay close attention. This is a special announcement.

After the Merger Publication, a New Lineup of Small Newspapers

The small newspapers in this city, under the responsible management of Director Feng of the Propaganda Department's Shanghai Office, were ordered to be adjusted and merged for publication in order to seek rational development. It is now known that the small newspapers have complied with the order and implemented the merger publication starting yesterday (1st). The new lineup of the merged small newspapers is revealed as follows: (1) The Seaport merges with the Telegraph, (2) The Power Daily merges with the Guangming Daily, (3) The Oriental Daily merges with the Shanghai Daily, (4) The Society Daily merges with the Xiong Daily, (5) The Shanghai Great News is changed to the Baojia Youth Organ Newspaper, (6) The Shanghai Daily is independent, (7) The Great News is independent, (8) The Robin Hood Shanghai Yue Opera Newspaper, the Drama Daily, and the Shen Opera Art Sea Daily are merged into the United Opera Newspaper, (9) The Lucky Daily, the Ten Thousand Words Newspaper, and the Peach Blossom News are merged into the Lucky Daily.

French Concession Bans the Sale of Fireworks

The French authorities have issued an order that, in order to maintain public security and order, the sale and setting off of firecrackers are absolutely prohibited within the French Concession.

Resolutions of the Shanghai West Security and Mutual Assistance Guidance Council: Unified Collection of Security and Mutual Assistance Expenses Commencing January 1st, Divided into Four Classes

The Shanghai West Security and Mutual Assistance Guidance Council, recognizing that the collection of security and mutual assistance expenses in the Shanghai West District in the past was handled separately by each joint security office, inevitably leading to irregularities, has, through its fifth meeting, passed a resolution to unify the collection method, entrusting the Shanghai West Office of the Finance Bureau to handle the collection. Hereafter, residents of Shanghai West, in addition to paying the aforementioned security and mutual assistance expenses, will not be required to pay other security and mutual assistance fees. It is reported that the collection of January's security and mutual assistance expenses commenced on the 1st. The monthly security and mutual assistance expenses for residents are divided into four classes: Special Class, three yuan; Class A, two yuan; Class B, one yuan; Class C, exempt.

Provisional Relief Center in Putuo District Continues Distribution of Relief Rice

The Provisional Relief Center in Putuo District was established this spring. Appreciating the urgency of the matter, enthusiastic individuals from all walks of life have actively sponsored and donated funds and rice to assist in providing porridge and emergency relief in this district. For half a month, over 30,000 people benefited. At the end of the emergency relief, there was a surplus of over 14,000 national currency units. A survey was then conducted of 284 impoverished households in the district, totaling 997 individuals, and 10,264 national currency units were distributed. The remaining 4,000 yuan was divided and sent to (1) Renji Infant Nursery, (2) Labor Hospital, (3) Pushan Villa, and (4) Jingye Nursing Home, 1,000 yuan each. Furthermore, Accountant Li Wenjie of Lixin Accounting Firm was requested to voluntarily and personally audit all accounts. There was a remaining surplus of 13 bags of broken rice, totaling 2,600 catties. The Board of Directors resolved to use it for winter relief. The other day, relief rice was distributed at the Jade Buddha Temple. A total of 1,190 impoverished residents in the district received one sheng of broken rice each, and an additional two yuan in savings currency was distributed to each person, totaling 2,380 yuan (this amount was raised by the directors through donations). Another 220-plus people who arrived later were also given one sheng of broken rice each. The work of the center is now complete, and it is announced that it will be concluded.

Shanghai Municipal Council's Chinese Children's Elementary School Changes Payment Date

The Shanghai Municipal Council's Information Office announces that the dates for paying tuition fees at the various Chinese children's elementary schools established by the Council were originally scheduled for February 8th and 9th. It has now been determined that the 8th is a regular holiday for the Council, and the office will be closed. Therefore, the payment dates for each elementary school have been changed to February 9th and 10th. Parents of students are requested to take note.

Enhancing Familial Happiness for Citizens: "Children's Happiness Week" Begins, Led by the Shanghai Municipal Council's Child Welfare Department, Ensuring Parents Gain Child-Rearing Knowledge

In order to allow residents of this port to obtain the joy of family, to stabilize social order, and to maintain the normal development of the future masters of the world, the Shanghai Municipal Council's Child Welfare Department is holding a "Children's Happiness Week" starting today, scheduled to conclude next Tuesday.

Increase in Cases of Lost Children

According to reporters, the reason for the Shanghai Municipal Council's launch of the Children's Happiness Movement is due to a particular increase in the number of children lost or running away from home. It has been found that a total of 912 such cases occurred last year, of which 635 cases were resolved satisfactorily through the efforts of the police. However, the whereabouts of the remaining children are still unknown. Therefore, the Shanghai Municipal Council's Child Welfare Department has launched a large-scale publicity campaign to seek the attention of parents and other guardians in this port.

Expanding Publicity and Child-Rearing Knowledge

During "Children's Happiness Week," the slogans and books for publicity are donated by the China Biochemical Pharmaceutical Factory at 32 Jiangxi Road. The methods of publicity include posting slogans on the walls of various roads, sending staff to give street lectures, broadcasting propaganda stories on the radio, and showing educational films in cinemas. The content of these slogans, lectures, stories, and films generally aims to provide parents with sufficient knowledge of child-rearing, not to excessively indulge children, and not to excessively apply harsh methods. According to an official of the Shanghai Municipal Council's Child Welfare Department who told reporters, the authorities hope that residents will not allow their young children to go out in the evenings, and hope that parents should weave their names and addresses on the clothes worn by their children with cotton yarn, so that in case of getting lost, the police can lead them back home. The authorities hope that the public will assist the Shanghai Municipal Council in handling this work. If a lost child is found crying in the street, an effort should be made to report it, in order to reduce the phenomenon of separation of families this year.

Shanghai West Impoverished People's Flour: Resale Again This Weekend

The first sale of flour for the impoverished people in the Shanghai West District was completed at the First Neighborhood on the day before yesterday (the 1st). As for the second sale of flour for the impoverished people, it is reported that it will begin on the 5th of this month (the first day of the lunar month) at the Second and Third Neighborhoods. Each certificate allows the purchase of two catties of flat flour, costing three yuan and sixty cents in legal tender.

Shanghai West Impoverished People's Association Obtains Subsidy from Relief Committee: Hundreds of Sets of Cotton Clothing, Funds of 50,000 Yuan

Last winter, the Shanghai West Impoverished People's Relief Association established a temporary shelter in Jinjia Lane to provide relief to impoverished people and beggars in the district, helping them to get through the harsh winter and avoid the suffering of sleeping in the open air. Poor people were admitted from 5:00 PM to 7:00 PM and left from 6:00 AM to 8:00 AM. Since its opening, the shelter has assisted no less than several hundred people. The other day, the association also obtained a subsidy of 50,000 yuan from the Shanghai Branch of the Central Relief Committee, and received donations of 351 sets of cotton clothing of various sizes.

Jinjia Lane Porridge Kitchen Has Started Distributing Porridge

The Jinjia Lane Porridge Kitchen, jointly sponsored by the Shanghai West Impoverished People's Relief Association of the World Red Swastika Society, started distributing porridge the day before yesterday (the 1st). The number of impoverished people in the district who heard the news and went to receive porridge was extremely enthusiastic, reaching over 500 people. For a time, impoverished people supported the old and led the young, arriving in an endless stream, and the situation was very good. It is reported that the amount of porridge distributed by the kitchen is one large bowl per person per day, equivalent to three ordinary rice bowls, and the density is also very high. The impoverished people in the district, after receiving it, were all visibly delighted.

The Shanghai Municipal Council's Schools Experienced an Unprecedented Increase in Student Numbers Last Year: Excerpt 6 from the Shanghai Municipal Council's Annual Report

Last year, the number of Chinese students wanting to attend Shanghai Municipal Council schools increased to an unprecedented level. Due to a lack of vacancies, some students could not be accommodated. The number of students in all day schools was 8,603 in December, of which 7,549 were Chinese and 1,054 were foreign. There were 1,386 students in all night schools. The classification of the Council's schools is as follows: (1) five Chinese public schools, (2) seven Chinese elementary schools, (3) four Western public schools, (4) four night schools. The tuition fees for each school were revised in September of the year before last, and continued to be implemented last year. Twenty-seven students in Chinese public schools received scholarships last year. Scholarship awards include full tuition waivers and free textbooks. In addition, the scholarship amount of 41 students, which was implemented in previous years, remained valid last year. A fee reduction program was implemented in Chinese elementary schools, stipulating that 10% of students in each school be exempt from tuition fees, and 5% be given a 50% reduction.

Situation of Each School is Good

(1) Chinese Public School: In the first half of last year, the school had a total of 607 registered students, increasing to 625 in the second half. The health of all students in the school was good, and their conduct was also excellent.

(2) Yucai Public School: In the first half of last year, there were 570 registered students, increasing to 579 in the second half. The health of the faculty and students of the school was generally satisfactory, and the school's discipline was also good.

(3) Nie Zhongcheng Public School: The school had 518 registered students in the first half of the year and 587 in the second half. In order to meet the needs of residents in the eastern district, the school's classes were expanded to 17. Students' attendance and health were excellent.

(4) Gezhi Public School: Last year, the school was still holding classes in temporary school buildings at 65 Daxi Road. The number of registered students in the first half of the year was 352, and 416 in the second half. The number of registered students in the first half of the year was not enthusiastic, perhaps because the situation in this port was uncertain at that time, and the school was far from the students' homes. Students' health was good. Students who were absent from class were mostly due to eye diseases and fever.

(5) Chinese Women's Middle School: There were 516 registered students in the first half of the year and 607 in the second half, exceeding the school's previous record for registered students.

(6) Chinese Elementary School: Last year, the Bureau maintained seven Chinese elementary schools, one elementary night school, and four other night schools. Among the seven Chinese elementary schools, three still operated on a half-day system, with some students attending classes in the morning and others in the afternoon. In the first half of last year, the seven Chinese elementary schools had 4,600 registered students, and 4,775 in the second half. There were 522 graduates. The health and attendance of each school were good.

The aforementioned elementary school night school is located within the Northern District Elementary School. Children from poor families who cannot attend day school due to economic reasons can attend the night school. The school had 369 students in the first half of the year and 381 in the second half.

The aforementioned four other night schools established by the Bureau include three for boys and one for girls. Each night school is located within a Chinese elementary school. There were 827 registered students in the first half of the year and 903 in the second half. Last year, applications from Chinese private schools for subsidies were separately reviewed by a special subcommittee of the Bureau's Education Committee. As a result, 120 schools were approved for grants, limited to those that could comply with the regulations of the Bureau's various departments. The total amount of subsidies approved was 625,000 yuan. Four schools were removed from the list of schools eligible for subsidies for various reasons.

Butchers at Renxian Bridge Vegetable Market Arrested for Raising Prices

Every year at the end of the lunar year, fresh goods and vegetable vendors all raise prices, taking the opportunity to profit. The pork stall at the Baxianqiao small vegetable market had pork prices raised to twenty-five yuan per catty. After investigation by the French Concession police, yesterday morning at around 9:30 AM, detectives were dispatched to arrest the owners of the pork stalls and take them to the police station for investigation. All of the pork was confiscated.
