Jiang Yilong Suddenly Retracts Confession in the Hua Liying Murder Case, Summons to All Witnesses, Retrial Postponed to Joint Collegiate Court

The sensational murder case of Hua Liying, a dancer at the MGM Ballroom, who was strangled to death on November 12 of last year by young men Zhang Hongsheng and Jiang Yilong for failing to borrow money, was solved and sent to the Second Special Court, which sentenced Zhang to fifteen years of imprisonment and Jiang to seven years. The law enforcement authorities and Shen Wenjie, chief prosecutor of the Second Special District Court, both filed appeals to the Third Branch Court, arguing that the initial trial was inappropriate. The two defendants also appealed, hiring lawyers. Yesterday, Cai Rixin, chief of the Criminal Division of the Third Branch of the High Court, sat in the Third Criminal Court to investigate the case. Zhang Hongsheng was defended by lawyers Wu Linkun, Wang Shuxun, and Shen E, while Jiang Yilong was defended by lawyer Wang Yigong. First, Zhang Hongsheng was interrogated. According to his statement, "The initial judgment said that I strangled the deceased with a tie because I failed to borrow money, which I cannot accept. I want you to know that I had been with the deceased, Hua Liying, for many years and spent a lot of money. Moreover, my family is wealthy, so there is no need to borrow money. I had a very good relationship with the deceased and had no intention of harming her. Therefore, I am appealing because I do not accept this." The official asked him to explain the whole story. Zhang replied, "I have known Jiang Yilong for three years. He is addicted to gambling. Although I often went with him, I never gambled.

Gambling During the Day, Dancing at Night

On the afternoon of the incident, I went to Xiyuan to gamble with Jiang. He lost three or four hundred yuan. In the evening, we went to the MGM Ballroom, where we met a classmate, Xie Shanxin, who was also acquainted with Hua Liying, and danced with Hua on the stage. At that time, Hua Liying told me that Xie often pestered her and prevented her from doing business, so she asked me to mediate and invited me to talk at her house. So, I went to Hua's house after the ballroom closed. When leaving the ballroom, Jiang Yilong asked me where I was going, and I explained the situation. Jiang wanted to go with me. When we got to Hua's house, Jiang asked me to borrow money from Hua, but I refused. He then opened his mouth to Hua himself, and she ridiculed him."

She Called for Help, I Pressed Her Mouth

"Jiang became angry out of humiliation, went forward and pushed Hua onto the bed. She called for help, so I went forward and pressed her mouth shut. She then scratched my face and neck with both hands. I got up and went to the dressing table to look at my face. In that instant, Jiang jumped onto the bed and strangled Hua with a tie. When I realized it and pulled Jiang away, Hua had already died. The official asked, 'Why did you stuff a towel into her lower body after strangling Hua?' He replied that it was actually done by Jiang and Zhang to avoid the ears and eyes of the detectives, indicating that the deceased had been forcibly raped without success. Later, Jiang also took out the jewelry and gave it to me.

Exchanged for Cash, Then Went to the Casino

The next day, after exchanging it for cash in various places, Jiang gambled and lost in the Nanshi casino. He still had 1,050 yuan left, which Jiang returned to me for Dr. Fan's medical expenses and loan shark debts." The official then asked, "Your statement says that Jiang Yilong wrote a letter stating that he did this. What is the situation?" He replied, "Because I was crying in the detention center, his conscience discovered it, so he told me not to cry. He wrote to his father to try to rescue me from prison. The letter stated that he had done this and asked his father to try to rescue us." Jiang Yilong's interrogation stated, "Although I wear a suit, the tie used to strangle Hua was not mine."

They Quarrelled, I Went Outside

"On November 12, Zhang and I went to the casino to gamble during the day. After going out, we went to the MGM Ballroom. After Zhang finished dancing with Hua, Zhang asked me to accompany him to Hua's house. I saw them talking and laughing as if 后, but suddenly they quarrelled, so I went outside." The official asked, "You admitted at the morgue that you conspired with Zhang to kill her. Why are you retracting your confession today?" Jiang replied, "Zhang asked me to admit it." The official also asked, "Did you write a letter to your father stating that you did this and asking your father to rescue Zhang Gong-sheng?" Jiang replied, "Zhang also asked me to write it. It was not my intention." Then, the court summoned the handling detective, the fathers of the two defendants, Wang Hongshi, the nanny employed by the victim, and Zhou Peide, who collected Hua Liying's body, to testify. Because it was already 7:30 PM, the court decided to postpone the case and reopen it for a joint collegiate court trial.

Chemical "Ammonium Sulfate" Fertilizer to Be Sold Throughout Central China, Already Adopted in North China Last Year

The chemical fertilizer required for Chinese farmland is all produced by the British firm Brunner Mond & Co. Therefore, since the outbreak of the Pacific War, the source has been cut off. As a result, the price of soybean cake, a domestic fertilizer, has recently soared, rising from 60-70 yuan to over 110 yuan. According to reporters, a large batch of chemical "ammonium sulfate" fertilizer will soon be shipped from Japan. Japan is a sulfur-producing country, and the military industry has been particularly developed recently, so the residue from the manufacture of gunpowder can be used to make fertilizer. North China has already adopted it last year, and this year it will be transported and sold to Central China. Therefore, the soybean cake market will gradually stabilize in the future.

Chen Qun Individually Funds the Establishment of the Nanjing Zecun Library

Construction of the Nanjing Zecun Library began in March of the 30th year of the Republic [1941], and was completed in February of the 31st year of the Republic [1942]. There are approximately 20,000 volumes of rare books and 40,000 volumes of Japanese "harmful" books, which are currently being sorted. It will open for reading in two months. The library's monthly recurring expenses are approximately 25,000 yuan, and it employs 48 staff members. It was founded by Mr. Chen Qun, and entirely funded by him personally. In Shanghai, a library has been built in the central area of the New Shanghai Municipality, completed in January of the 31st year of the Republic [1942], covering an area of ten mu. The Shanghai Postal Administration issued Notice No. 1773 yesterday, stating that airmail items sent to various rear areas via China National Aviation Corporation are uniformly charged per ten grams as a weight unit. Regarding the airmail rates for letters and postcards, which were previously set at 2.5 jiao per weight unit as per the Bureau's Notice No. 1649 issued on February 1, 1941, it has been found that from February 1 of this year, the airmail rates for letters will be changed to one yuan in Central Reserve Bank notes per weight unit (ten grams). The airmail rates for airmail items mutually sent within the peace zone via China National Aviation Corporation (see Notice 1752) remain unchanged. This notice is hereby issued for public knowledge.

Free Talk

The Teacher Speaks of Himself - The Edge of Life and Death

— Jing Ling

My wife's abdomen is gradually swelling, and my eye sockets are slowly sinking. My wife understands my sorrow, and she sighs all day long. Life is so pressing, life is so difficult. The little life is lurking in her belly, and a tragic fate has already been arranged.

My monthly salary is difficult to cover the living expenses of my wife and me. We live in a pigeon cage-like attic, eat watery porridge, and wear old clothes with countless holes. I often confess to my wife that I feel sorry for her. Tearful eyes often meet. I say that I am too weak, but she also complains about her own incompetence, unable to share the burden of this small family.

Living beyond our means has become a daily routine, and the pawnshop has become a familiar acquaintance. The northwest wind blows incessantly, and the cold pricks make my teeth chatter. The thin jacket is still waving in the wind...

Seeing me coming home with books and papers, constantly trembling, my wife's eyes are filled with tears again.

The next day, while I was at school teaching, my wife pawned her only cotton robe and redeemed my cotton robe. The money was not enough, so she borrowed from the sister-in-law upstairs. When I came back, I saw her wearing a jacket and blouse, and doubts arose in my heart. My nose felt sour, and I remained silent. She had already taken the cotton robe for me to put on.

After she put it on for me, feeling a little warmer, she comforted me and wiped away my tears, touching her cold fingers, my tears welled up even more.

The oil pressing queue snaked through the streets. A ruthless whip fell on people's heads, and a burst of screams shook the queue. How difficult it is to continue life! I wanted to lower my head and not look at the reality in front of me, but a kind of inexplicable emotion gnawed at my heart.

Walking into the attic, turning on the light, preparing to grade some papers, reading the children's innocent and pure words, perfect ideals, living beautifully like in heaven, they have no filth and suffering.

Just as my thoughts flew over ten years, a heavy and slow footstep on the stairs awakened my memory. I have only walked twenty-seven years on the road of life, and the past happiness seems to have been decades ago.

What is present before my eyes is my wife's disheveled hair and two dull, lifeless eyes, putting down the empty bottle next to the bed, pressing one hand on her abdomen and falling onto the bed, murmuring:

"Ling! I'm in some pain..."

I was stunned. It's only been eight months. How can I cope? I stood there like a wooden chicken. My wife tugged at me...

Two inexperienced people stared at each other, looking at my wife's face. I counted the banknotes in my pocket, piecing together less than ten yuan. I helped my wife to lie down more comfortably and ran downstairs to the school...

Walking into the principal's office, the principal was reading the newspaper, looking at me sideways through his glasses, as if surprised, feeling that my arrival was abrupt. I opened my mouth but then shrank back. I remembered that I had already drawn two months' salary in advance. Finally, braving great courage, I opened my mouth:

"Principal, my wife is about to give birth. Please allow me to borrow two months' salary."

"Haven't you already drawn two months in advance? I think you know the school's financial situation very well. The price of salt rises with the sun, and you are already an exception, drawing two months in advance, and now..."

"When I came out, she was already in severe abdominal pain. Please help me especially, because I am really in a hurry..."

Seeing how anxious I was, he leisurely tapped the pencil on the cup a few times. I couldn't help but get angry and turned around to run out. He sneered behind me:

"Heh... Giving birth to a child is not easy..."

I heard him but didn't argue with him, and pleaded with Uncle Wang, the gatekeeper, explaining my urgent matter. He generously lent me twenty yuan, and I ran straight home as if flying.

Rushing upstairs, my wife was in even more severe pain. The sister-in-law upstairs was carrying an oil bottle and said to me directly:

"Sir, your wife injured herself pressing oil. You shouldn't have let her go. She is so pregnant. You men don't take care of women. It's the same with my man." She gestured and started giving medical advice, blaming the men. I could only say to my wife:

"I think I should ask a doctor to come and have a look first!"

My wife was in too much pain to respond. I went out without thinking, borrowed the neighbor's phone and called the obstetrics hospital.

The doctor came, and my wife screamed loudly in pain. After examining her, the doctor told me to prepare hot water. I looked at my wife and had to take the hot water bottle to make hot water. When I came back from the tiger stove, the door was closed. I heard my wife's groans, and then I heard a low and high-pitched sound. I knew that a small life had arrived in the suffering human world...

At noon, I went home and walked into the attic. My wife was breastfeeding the baby. The baby was very small, and the two small eyes were very bright, desperately sucking on the nipple. The scarcity of milk made the mother even more painful. My wife frowned and looked at the little thing. I kissed him with pity. My wife was afraid of making him cry and pushed me away. I asked my wife:

"Can milk powder be fed to him?"

"I think I should eat and drink more, and the milk will be more plentiful!" I felt a surge of love and warmth from being a mother, warming my heart.

Taking the rice jar to cook porridge, there was not enough rice for even one meal of porridge. I secretly took it to cook it, letting my wife eat more, and I only drank half a bowl of porridge soup. My wife asked me if I was full, and I said I was full.

Some friends generously helped me find ways to get money and bought rice and vegetables for my wife to eat. My wife is very clean. The sister-in-law upstairs often helped her wash some dirty clothes, but she had many children, so my wife felt bad and secretly washed them herself without telling me.

Once, twice, she caught a cold, got sick, and had a high fever again. The sister-in-law upstairs saw me and warned me:

"Sir! A fever is not good for your wife. Be careful!"

I tried desperately to borrow money to ask a doctor to examine her, but doctor's fees and medicine seemed to be the exclusive property of the rich, and we had no share. Heavens! How wide is the distance between life and death? (Proceeds will be used for scholarship aid)

Review of "The Simpleton's Love History"

— Liu Chang

Just looking at the silly appearance of Wang Er (the protagonist of the film) wearing tortoiseshell glasses reminds one of Roscoe Arbuckle. And "The Simpleton's Love History" is indeed a slapstick comedy with a Roscoe Arbuckle flavor.

The story tells of Sugiyama Fumio, who, following his mother's words, takes his first ancestor Sugiyama Daisaku as a model, and wholeheartedly wants to relive the ancestor's experiences today. However, the past is the past. How can such things be recreated now? So he, like Don Quixote, suffered a lot of ridicule and mockery. However, the fool has his own luck, and he actually survives in desperate situations, gains advantages everywhere, and finally wins the favor of the daughter of the manager of a product company, and they set off together to Manchuria for an inspection trip.

As mentioned above, the story is quite interesting. If the contrast between the past and the present can be emphasized, and many jokes can be unearthed in the middle, and then a romance is added, writing about the crowd's mockery of Sugiyama Fumio and the manager's daughter Hiroko's sincere love for him... In this way, it could become a satirical comedy, that is certain. However, after watching "The Simpleton's Love History," I feel that the screenwriter and director have failed such a good subject.

In film art, the "speed" and "consistency" of camera cuts are the first things to pay attention to. In terms of content and awareness of American films, don't worry about it first; at least, they pay very close attention to the grasp of emotions. That is to say, they are very good at understanding the tricks of taking the long and supplementing the short, simplifying the complex, and using jump-cut shots to tightly hold the audience's heartstrings from beginning to end. In this way, it often makes old ladies who are not used to watching movies feel as if they have fallen into a fog of five miles, feeling inexplicable, but more importantly, it fully demonstrates the characteristics of modern film art.

"The Simpleton's Love History" is not very sufficient in these points. According to the overall count, there are no less than four or five battle scenes in this film, each lasting no less than seven or eight minutes, so half of the film is taken up. In old novels, when Zhang Fei met Ma Chao, they fought one round after another, and the author could follow along and describe one round after another. But in movies, this is completely unnecessary.

On the contrary, some places make people feel too hasty. Perhaps because unnecessary descriptions take up too much space, many shots can only see some figures wriggling, someone goes out, someone comes in, like a revolving lantern, letting the director control the plot. When the plot is over, the movie is over. But the strength of a slapstick comedy is definitely not in narrating the plot. It should use many concrete actions, tones, deeds... to create jokes and move the audience.

Also, since the story contrasts ancient and modern times, then, obviously, the ancient part should occupy less space, and the modern part should occupy more, and the two should be organically linked together. Although this film also pays attention to this point, I think the ancient part can still be largely deleted. On the contrary, more shots of Sugiyama Fumio and Hiroko falling in love should be added. (Hiroko has almost no scenes in the film).

There is also a small flaw, that is, the section where he dreams of catching thieves later. Dreaming easily makes people suspect that it is real. The director does not seem to have treated the dream world and reality differently.

In short, "The Simpleton's Love History" is a work worth watching. But to criticize it seriously, there are still many uneven and uneven places, and the director is asked to pay attention to them.

Seeking a Full Meal in Winter

— Jing Bao Ke

The Teacher

— Written by James Hilton, Translated by Yi Jin

(10) (1)

All the above passed through his mind in a moment of protest and anger, but he didn't say a word of it. He only straightened his tattered robe and walked away a few steps, "Ahem—ahem." He had argued enough. At the door, he turned around and said: "I—ahem—don't want to resign—you do—ahem—what you want with the matter!"

Chips turned to look back at that scene of more than twenty years ago, and couldn't help feeling a little sorry for Alston in his heart. Especially because Ralston had no idea what forces he was dealing with. Even Chips himself was like that regarding this matter. Neither of them correctly estimated the strength of the Brookfield tradition, and its determination to protect itself and its protectors. Because things happened by chance: that morning, there was a student waiting to see Ralston, and he happened to hear all the conversation between the two of them inside outside the door; he was of course very nervous when he heard these words, and told his friends. Some of them, in a surprisingly short period of time, told their parents: therefore, soon everyone knew that Ralston had insulted Chips and asked Chips to resign. The result of this development was a surge of sympathy and bias that Chips had never dreamed of in advance. He felt it was simply shocking that Ralston had completely lost people's hearts; he was respected and feared, but not liked; in this matter of Chips, his being disliked even exceeded his being respected and feared. Some people were talking about that if Ralston really drove Chips away, there would inevitably be a disturbance in the school. Many of the teachers in the school were young people, who usually thought that Chips was unbearably old-fashioned, but now they also supported him, because they hated Ralston's kind of driving slave thorns and saw in this old teacher a style of not fearing the strong. One day, Sir John Rivers, the chairman of the board of directors, visited Brookfiled without notifying Ralston and went directly to Chips' place. (29)

A Few Words

— Yi Wen

If I could be reborn, I would practice patience and never be hindered by difficulties.

The result of patience can match genius, as the saying goes: "There are only two creatures that can surpass the pyramids (that is, do difficult work), namely, eagles and snails (referring to talented people and patient people)."

If I could be reborn, I would cultivate courage, for courage is the most kind and weakness is the most cruel in the world (the courageous have a small heart, while the cowardly bully the weak).

If I could be reborn, I would always be optimistic, life is like a mirror, if you laugh at it, it also laughs at you; if you frown at it, it also repays you in the same way.

Inner joy not only warms yourself, but this warmth will also enter the people we come into contact with. (Returns a reward) Social Service

Reader's Letter Launches Spring Festival One Yuan Charity Movement

Editor:

The weather has suddenly turned cold in the past few days. When I sleep at night, I cover myself with two quilts and still complain about being cold! But looking back at the homeless men, women, old and young people on the streets, not only do they have no home to return to, but they also don't even have three meals a day. Then, if this continues, won't they just be heading towards the road to death? We are all human beings and should love others. We cannot watch our poor compatriots suffer from hunger and cold, and even die on the roadside. In this chaotic world, we should bring out our conscience and do some relief work. I think your newspaper, with the purpose of serving society, will definitely be happy to launch it!

Now I have proposed a method, which is that during the Spring Festival period, enthusiastic staff members from various stores will voluntarily save money and donate. As for the amount of the donation, each person only needs to donate one yuan. If the store has a population of ten people, then ten yuan will be donated. After this donation is automatically collected, it will be handed over to your newspaper for safekeeping, and then your newspaper will forward it to charitable organizations. After the charitable organizations receive it, they will hold charity events such as distributing porridge and clothes. I think that such a method is only a small expense for the donors, but it is a great gospel for the general compatriots in distress! At the same time, it is also the benefactors creating boundless blessings. The above is just my humble opinion, and I hope your newspaper will further solicit donations. I am also a store employee, and I would like to donate five yuan first as a prelude. Sincerely, the initiator, Anonymous

Children Save Candy Money to Purchase Cotton Clothing Vouchers for Distribution

(Original letter) We read your newspaper's supplement every morning, which appeals for the poor and is very moving. We will use the candy money we usually save to purchase cotton clothing vouchers. In addition to distributing them ourselves, we still have fifteen left, and we request that you distribute them on our behalf. Shi Ronglin and Rongming (Editor's note: We will certainly comply)

School News

(1) The Pude Association at 8 Wenzhou Road has been running a short-term compulsory elementary school and a compulsory night school for the masses for two years. The level ranges from lower grades to upper grades. Tuition and miscellaneous fees are completely free, and books and stationery are provided.

(2) The Poor Children's Elementary School on Robison Road, Shanghai West, completely waives tuition and miscellaneous fees. There are currently more than 300 students. It is now scheduled to enroll students of all grades within days.

(3) The Alumni Association of the First Vocational Supplementary School is offering student loans. All students who have graduated or studied at the school, if they wish to continue their studies at the school but are unable to pay the tuition fees, may apply for student loans from the Alumni Association of this school. There are still balances remaining, so apply quickly.

Introduction to Free Clinics and Medication

(4) Mr. Shi Langming wrote: I would like to introduce that the Second Special District Social Service Department of the Shanghai Special City Party Headquarters of the Chinese Kuomintang has set up two free clinics some time ago. The Western Medicine Department is located at 93, Lane 482, Caishi Road, French Concession, headed by Dr. Fang Mingxu. The Traditional Chinese Medicine Department is located within the headquarters of our party at 12, Lane 153, Beiler Road. The organization is perfect, and medicine is completely free. Residents of the French Concession only need to obtain a free clinic voucher from the head of the village or the head of the Jia where they live to go to any of the above-mentioned clinics for medical treatment; if there is no free clinic voucher, those with sufficient proof are limited to outpatient services for free. This method can be enjoyed by all hidden poor compatriots.
